<div id="review_682632412" class="review nosyndicate" itemprop="reviews" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Review">
  <link itemprop="url" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/682632412" />
    <a title="Rosalinda *KRASNORADA*" class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/12788865-rosalinda-krasnorada"><img alt="Rosalinda *KRASNORADA*" src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1583582487p2/12788865.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/682632412?book_show_action=true">Jul 31, 2013</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="Rosalinda *KRASNORADA*" class="user" itemprop="url" name="Rosalinda *KRASNORADA*" href="/user/show/12788865-rosalinda-krasnorada">Rosalinda *KRASNORADA*</a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="it was amazing"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">it was amazing</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span></span>

          <span class="greyText">&nbsp;&middot;&nbsp;</span>
          <a class="lightGreyText" title="Kindle Edition " href="/book/show/17978680-unteachable">review of another edition</a>


        

          <div class="uitext greyText bookshelves">
            Shelves:
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/12788865-rosalinda-krasnorada?shelf=perfect-hero-and-heroine">perfect-hero-and-heroine</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/12788865-rosalinda-krasnorada?shelf=favorites">favorites</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/12788865-rosalinda-krasnorada?shelf=best-ya-book-ever">best-ya-book-ever</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/12788865-rosalinda-krasnorada?shelf=made-me-cry">made-me-cry</a>
          </div>
    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer682632412" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer11224675921070444134"><br/><br/><b> MISSION FUCKING ACCOMPLISHED!!!</b><br/><br/> <img src='https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1381655864i/5149745._SX540_.jpg' class='gr-hostedUserImg'/> <br/><br/>Trying to write a coherent review of a book you read more than one month ago SUCKS. Thanks God there are amazing reviews out there that you could read that will completely convince you to read this book. But to be honest, you don’t need to be convinced. This is one of those books that will rock your world.<br/><br/>Following my ‘hell to the no spoilers policy’ I’m just going to say very little about this story.<br/><br/>Maise and Evan meet in a Carnival and they share a special mom</span>
  <span id="freeText11224675921070444134" style="display:none"><br><br><b> MISSION FUCKING ACCOMPLISHED!!!</b><br><br> <img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1381655864i/5149745._SX540_.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg"> <br><br>Trying to write a coherent review of a book you read more than one month ago SUCKS. Thanks God there are amazing reviews out there that you could read that will completely convince you to read this book. But to be honest, you don’t need to be convinced. This is one of those books that will rock your world.<br><br>Following my ‘hell to the no spoilers policy’ I’m just going to say very little about this story.<br><br>Maise and Evan meet in a Carnival and they share a special moment together.<br><br><b>
  <blockquote>”You’re pretty brave, sitting up front by yourself”</blockquote>
</b><br><br>Days later they realize they are going to spend a whole year together because Evan is Maise’s new teacher. Nope, this is not just another teacher-student book. This one is way different and special because the story is not about being scared and denying your feelings just because the right thing to do is staying away from your student. <b>This is a book about FEELINGS. About growing up even though we don’t grow up, we just get bigger and older, right?</b><br><br>This is a book about imperfect people, people with flaws but not weak people. People who want to LIVE, 18 years old teens who know what they want in life and more importantly know what they don’t want. About making mistakes and running away from them, about believing even though when you believe in something you have hopes and life can crush them.<br><br>And this is a book about friendship. About friends that can get a wrong idea, friends that can fail because friends are not perfect, we can all disappoint our friends and it’s still ok, it’s not the end of the world!<br><br><b>
  <blockquote>“You’re never saying what you think you’re saying”</blockquote>
</b><br><br>This is a book about LOVE. In all its meaning. Love for life, for someone special, for a friend, for your fucked up mother even if she doesn’t deserve it… just LOVE and FAITH.<br><br><b>
  <blockquote>
<br>"I shut my eyes and all the world drops dead;<br>I lift my lids and all is born again.<br>(I think I made you up inside my head.)<br>The stars go waltzing out in blue and red,<br>And arbitrary blackness gallops in:<br>I shut my eyes and all the world drops dead.<br>I dreamed that you bewitched me into bed<br>And sung me moon-struck, kissed me quite insane.<br>(I think I made you up inside my head.)<br>God topples from the sky, hell's fires fade:<br>Exit seraphim and Satan's men:<br>I shut my eyes and all the world drops dead.<br>I fancied you'd return the way you said,<br>But I grow old and I forget your name.<br>(I think I made you up inside my head.)<br>I should have loved a thunderbird instead;<br>At least when spring comes they roar back again.<br>I shut my eyes and all the world drops dead.<br>(I think I made you up inside my head.)"<br>
</blockquote>
</b><br><br>And this is a book about having guts to pursue what you want, what you believe in. About taking the risk and not looking back (ni para coger carrerilla as we would say in Spanish).<br><br><b>
  <blockquote>“Every dream is a pipe dream before someone achieves it”</blockquote>
</b><br><br>So don’t even give it a second thought, just buy it and enjoy this AMAZING ROLLER COASTER. <br><br>Obrigada, Ana Rita, for your great rec xxx<br><br>P.S. BTW, about the ending... DO NOT OPEN THE SPOILER IF YOU HAVEN'T READ THIS GEM! <a class="jsShowSpoiler spoilerAction">(view spoiler)</a><span class="spoilerContainer" style="display: none">[ I've read this was a NON HEA ending. Seriously? Did we all read the same book? Ladies, we all read books so we all have imagination, right? The end was perfect and in my opinion I didn't need an Epilogue about them 10 years later being married and with kids, that's boring.  <a class="jsHideSpoiler spoilerAction">(hide spoiler)</a>]</span><br><br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1381655864ra/5149746.gif" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></span>

<div id="review_1080335421" class="review" itemprop="reviews" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Review">
  <link itemprop="url" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/1080335421" />
    <a title="Angela" class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/30035966-angela"><img alt="Angela" src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1523817330p2/30035966.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/1080335421?book_show_action=true">Oct 14, 2014</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="Angela" class="user" itemprop="url" name="Angela" href="/user/show/30035966-angela">Angela</a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="it was amazing"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">it was amazing</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span></span>



        

          <div class="uitext greyText bookshelves">
            Shelves:
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/30035966-angela?shelf=badass-females">badass-females</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/30035966-angela?shelf=5-star-favorites">5-star-favorites</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/30035966-angela?shelf=read-it-and-weep">read-it-and-weep</a>
          </div>
    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer1080335421" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer4023409736081066669"><b> Why has it taken me so long to post my review??</b><br/><i>“Part of falling in love with someone is actually falling in love with yourself. Realizing that you're gorgeous, you're fearless and unpredictable, you're a firecracker spitting light, entrancing a hundred faces that stare up at you with starry eyes.” </i><br/><br/><b>What did you just do to me Leah Raeder?!?! Was my heart just beautifully broken?? I think so. </b><br/><br/><i>Unteachable</i> is about a student and a teacher falling hopelessly in love. <b>Emphasis on the hopeless part.</b> Sa</span>
  <span id="freeText4023409736081066669" style="display:none"><b> Why has it taken me so long to post my review??</b><br><i>“Part of falling in love with someone is actually falling in love with yourself. Realizing that you're gorgeous, you're fearless and unpredictable, you're a firecracker spitting light, entrancing a hundred faces that stare up at you with starry eyes.” </i><br><br><b>What did you just do to me Leah Raeder?!?! Was my heart just beautifully broken?? I think so. </b><br><br><i>Unteachable</i> is about a student and a teacher falling hopelessly in love. <b>Emphasis on the hopeless part.</b> Saying that Maise is an average teen would be a lie. Forced to grow up at an early age and take care of herself, she sees things different than most people her age. She also seeks out older male lovers to fill the void of a male figure in her life since her father left her. A void that she says "can only be filled with dick.". Maise is a ball of cocky attitude and insecurities. She is a character that you wouldn't think you would find funny, but with her F this attitude you'll find yourself loving her. As far as NA protagonist go she feels more real than any other leading ladies I've met recently. <br><a href="http://1.bp.blogspot.com/-egHm4TVlF34/VGgg0kozvdI/AAAAAAAAAaU/qHHRwJrz3fU/s1600/f%2Bthis.gif" rel="nofollow noopener">
  <img height="160" src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1451477338ra/17547767.gif" width="320" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</a><br><div>
<br><br>After a steamy evening at the carnival with a man who instantly takes her breath away she discovers him to be her new film teacher. Instead of calling things off they take to seeing how far they can push their relationship. <br><br>Mr. Evan Wilke is the 32-year-old heartthrob teacher that was all passion and mystery. Despite finding out that he is her teacher he can't stay away from her. They end up sneaking school make-out sessions and hot mini sexy getaways together. Evan is all sorts of adorable. I'm use to the leading males in NA novels being cocky, rude, and a lot of times controlling. It was refreshing to have him be the super vulnerable one. He had me hardcore swooning with his way with words so much during this book.<br><br><i>“...You should love something while you have it, love it fully and without reservation, even if you know you'll lose it someday. We lose everything. If you're trying to avoid loss, there's no point in taking another breath, or letting your heart beat one more time. It all ends." His fingers curl around mine. "That's all life is. Breathing in, breathing out. The space between two breaths.” </i> <br><br><b>Seriously, stop being so perfect and breaking my heart Evan! </b><br><br>As the relationship builds and as the characters spend more time together you start to slowly question the motives of the relationship. You are left wondering what's keeping their relationship going. Is it the love or the forbidden-ness that is holding it together? Along with the amazingly built characters came the wonderfully lyrical written romance scenes. And there are A LOT of steamy scenes in this book. <br><br><a href="http://4.bp.blogspot.com/-HKuUG9k76Z4/VGgtouTyduI/AAAAAAAAAak/pGNxuIwO-No/s1600/11877185.gif" rel="nofollow noopener"><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1416117879ra/11893497.gif" class="gr-hostedUserImg"></a><br>My face basically looked like this the whole time.<br><br>We're talking next level hot. <br>As much as I loved the two main characters this story did however have a few flaws. Towards the middle of this book the story kind of drifts too this odd side story. It involves her mom and some random side characters, Hiyam and Park. I really didn't enjoy any of them. I wanted to feel a little more connection to her mother, but was left wanting more. Even knowing the connection would be one of negativeness I still wanted it. I did love when she finally starts to take control of her life and tells off her B of a mom.<br><br><i> She stared at some central point on my face, not quite my eyes. "This how I raised you? To make fuckin' threats about disowning me?" "No," I said quietly. "This is how <b>I</b> raised me." </i><br><br><b>Hey mom, need some help with that BURN! </b><br><br>The side character I did like was Wesley. He was so cute and I was hoping him and Maise would end up together. The witty and real dialogue they zap back and forth between each other is amazing. The plot of this story was so strong that it more than made up for the few tiny flaws. Even though I figured out the "big twist" before it happened the way it was presented still had me flipping and failing everywhere screaming <i>"NOOO!! I DIDN'T WANT IT TO BE REAL! WHY DID I HAVE TO BE RIGHT!!! WHY???!!"</i><br><a href="http://1.bp.blogspot.com/-7aZhkz7MyQk/VGg1LAx3EQI/AAAAAAAAAa0/HOB9O8RBaCI/s1600/11582702.gif" rel="nofollow noopener"><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1451478095ra/17547850.gif" class="gr-hostedUserImg"></a>
</div><br><br>Laeder's writing style was amazing, breathtaking, and unforgettable. The way she perfectly twisted in a movie theme, that now has me loving Casablanca even more, and the way Maise uses past tense in her mind was something I found so interesting. The ending of this story left me with so many feelings. It gave me the perfect combination of wanting more and being completely satisfied. This might have (even from my description) sounded like just another F'd up love story, but it was so much more than that. It was of loneliness, desperation, and about how hard it is to grow up. If you're a fan of Colleen Hoover's <i>Slammed</i> or Tabitha Suzma's <i>Forbidden</i> then you'll love Unteachable.<br><br><b>READ THIS REVIEW AND OTHERS OVER ON OUR BLOG:<br><b><a href="http://southernbredsouthernread.blogspot.com/" rel="nofollow noopener"><br></a></b><br><b><a href="http://southernbredsouthernread.blogspot.com/" rel="nofollow noopener">SBSR SBSR SBSR </a></b><br><b><a href="http://southernbredsouthernread.blogspot.com/" rel="nofollow noopener">SBSR SBSR SBSR</a></b><br><b><a href="http://southernbredsouthernread.blogspot.com/" rel="nofollow noopener">SBSR SBSR SBSR </a></b></b></span>
  <a data-text-id="4023409736081066669" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

          </span>

<div id="review_680786557" class="review nosyndicate" itemprop="reviews" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Review">
  <link itemprop="url" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/680786557" />
    <a title="Kristin (KC) - Traveling Sister" class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/4971692-kristin-kc---traveling-sister"><img alt="Kristin (KC) - Traveling Sister" src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1486056026p2/4971692.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/680786557?book_show_action=true">Jul 29, 2013</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="Kristin (KC) - Traveling Sister" class="user" itemprop="url" name="Kristin (KC) - Traveling Sister" href="/user/show/4971692-kristin-kc---traveling-sister">Kristin (KC) - Traveling Sister</a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="really liked it"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">really liked it</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span></span>

          <span class="greyText">&nbsp;&middot;&nbsp;</span>
          <a class="lightGreyText" title="Kindle Edition " href="/book/show/17978680-unteachable">review of another edition</a>


        

          <div class="uitext greyText bookshelves">
            Shelves:
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/4971692-kristin-kc---traveling-sister?shelf=forbidden-love">forbidden-love</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/4971692-kristin-kc---traveling-sister?shelf=young-adult">young-adult</a>
          </div>
    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer680786557" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer17802961443903133246"><b>*4 Stars!*</b><br/><br/>This gripping story has a <b>tragic beauty</b> that is not easily defined. It doesn't offer a black and white scenario that tells you how to feel and where you stand—but instead presents varying shades of grey that invite you to think and decide for yourself. Some may question its morality or criticize its content, but no one can deny that this story boldly braves the controversial—generously offering us the excitement and allure of an intense forbidden love!<br/><br/><i>
  <b>
    <blockquote>I see the lights every nig</blockquote></b></i></span>
  <span id="freeText17802961443903133246" style="display:none"><b>*4 Stars!*</b><br><br>This gripping story has a <b>tragic beauty</b> that is not easily defined. It doesn't offer a black and white scenario that tells you how to feel and where you stand—but instead presents varying shades of grey that invite you to think and decide for yourself. Some may question its morality or criticize its content, but no one can deny that this story boldly braves the controversial—generously offering us the excitement and allure of an intense forbidden love!<br><br><i>
  <b>
    <blockquote>I see the lights every night. It seems like the whole world has figured out how to be happy, but no one's letting me in on the secret.</blockquote>
  </b>
</i><br><i>Unteachable</i> kicks off with an in-your-face reality. We meet <b>Maise</b>, an eighteen year old emotionally numb high school senior suffering the heartbreaking affects of her neglectful, drug-addicted mother. Maise uses men and sex to hide from herself, temporarily gaining an empty confidence from the attention. When she meets <b>Evan</b>, her dead world starts to come to life. But dating her equally broken teacher will prove to be...complicated. <br><br><b>
  <i>
    <blockquote>I can't hold on to you. You're like that shooting star. Just a trail of fire in my hands.</blockquote>
  </i>
</b><br>I'd be lying if I said this story didn't dramatically play on each and every one of my emotions. The author uses such an artful, insightful articulation, that I often found myself rereading many quotes, letting them marinate in my mind. <br><br>For me, this book was all about its amazing, badass heroine. Evan was a sweet hero, but his character felt almost empty, and never truly thrived. It was Maise who completely stole the show! As damaged as she appeared, Maise was incredibly funny, with an entertaining inner dialogue filled with dry humor and quick wit. She made me feel her despair and heartache, and then she made me see her <i>worth</i>. Her inspiring character was an excellent portrayal of a confused, lost, and lonely girl gaining some perspective on life. <br><br>There <i>were</i> some moments, particularly mid-story, that became somewhat redundant, leaving me scrounging for more depth. However, the unique and realistic writing style made up for what the plot seemed to lack. It had a raw <b>power</b> that snuck up on me. Don't be deceived by the natural feel of the dialogue; although its structure may appear choppy at times, I found it served well to emphasize the delivery. The story was expressed poetically, sprinkled with dramatic pauses and intentional fragmentations. I loved that its prose mimicked the 'film-producing, movie-making' theme. The storytelling was captivating, insightful, and easily became an addiction as it brought many beautifully touching moments to life. <br><br><br>*I'll end by quoting some pretty solid advice*...<i>
  <b>
    <blockquote>"You should love something while you have it, love it fully and without reservation, even if you know you'll lose it someday. We lose everything. If you're trying to avoid loss, there's no point in taking another breath, or letting your heart beat one more time. It all ends. That's all life is. Breathing in, breathing out. The space between two breaths." </blockquote>
  </b>
</i><br><a href="http://tinypic.com?ref=2mh7uop" target="_blank" rel="nofollow noopener">
  <img height="50" width="50" src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1380347313i/701667.jpg" alt="Image and video hosting by TinyPic" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</a><b>
  <u>Book Stats:</u>
</b><br><b>▪	 Genre/Category:</b> Romance/New Adult<br><b>▪	 Steam Caliber:</b> Maximum, generous steam!<br><b>▪ Romance:</b> Quick connection. Forbidden love. <br><b>▪	 Characters:</b> Broken but kickass, hilarious heroine. Sweet, damaged hero. <br><b>▪	 Plot:</b> Teacher/student relationship.<br><b>▪ Writing:</b> Deep, insightful, humorous, and lyrical. <br><b>▪ POV:</b> 1st Person: Heroine<br><b>▪	 Cliffhanger:</b> None/Standalone<br><br><a href="http://prettywordsbookblog.com" rel="nofollow noopener">
  <img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1412050368i/11316768.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</a><br><br><a href="https://www.facebook.com/pages/Pretty-Words-Book-Blog/860331017317983" rel="nofollow noopener">
  <img height='“40"' width="150" src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1413062455i/11461733._SX540_.png" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</a></span>

<div id="review_679929829" class="review" itemprop="reviews" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Review">
  <link itemprop="url" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/679929829" />
    <a title="Duchess Nicole" class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/2204947-duchess-nicole"><img alt="Duchess Nicole" src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1499265843p2/2204947.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/679929829?book_show_action=true">Jul 28, 2013</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="Duchess Nicole" class="user" itemprop="url" name="Duchess Nicole" href="/user/show/2204947-duchess-nicole">Duchess Nicole</a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="it was amazing"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">it was amazing</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span></span>

          <span class="greyText">&nbsp;&middot;&nbsp;</span>
          <a class="lightGreyText" title="Kindle Edition " href="/book/show/17978680-unteachable">review of another edition</a>


          <div>
    <span class="greyText">Recommended to Duchess Nicole by: </span>
      <a href="/user/show/4398001-nicole">Nicole </a>
  </div>


          <div class="uitext greyText bookshelves">
            Shelves:
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/2204947-duchess-nicole?shelf=genre-contemp-romance">genre-contemp-romance</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/2204947-duchess-nicole?shelf=5-star-read">5-star-read</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/2204947-duchess-nicole?shelf=favorites">favorites</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/2204947-duchess-nicole?shelf=e-pcs">e-pcs</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/2204947-duchess-nicole?shelf=genre-new-adult">genre-new-adult</a>
          </div>
    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer679929829" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer16060699226195922564"><b>
  <blockquote>"You should love something while you have it, love it fully and without reservation, even if you know you'll lose it someday. We lose everything. If you're trying to avoid loss, there's no point in taking another breath, or letting your heart beat one more time. It all ends...That's all life is. Breathing in, breathing out. The space between two breaths."</blockquote>
</b><br/><br/>Boy, did I fight this book with everything in me. But Leah Raeder dragged my sorry ass kicking and screaming into the book fantasy ether, a</span>
  <span id="freeText16060699226195922564" style="display:none"><b>
  <blockquote>"You should love something while you have it, love it fully and without reservation, even if you know you'll lose it someday. We lose everything. If you're trying to avoid loss, there's no point in taking another breath, or letting your heart beat one more time. It all ends...That's all life is. Breathing in, breathing out. The space between two breaths."</blockquote>
</b><br /><br />Boy, did I fight this book with everything in me. But Leah Raeder dragged my sorry ass kicking and screaming into the book fantasy ether, and I was LOST. I'm not quite sure if I got out of it what everyone else got out of it...I'm not even sure if I can say that I LIKED it all. The content was too much for me...I felt very uncomfortable at first. But it was like reading a book about war...you know you don't like the CONTENT. The <i>story</i>, however, and the <i>telling</i>...are so engaging and so tragic that you are mesmerized. And I was, completely <b>riveted.</b><br /><br /><b>
  <u>MY SYNOPSIS:</u>
</b><br />Maise O'Malley is an eighteen year old girl living a rough life. And we're not talking crazy twisted...she simply has it hard. Her father doesn't exist, her mother is an alcoholic, a drug addict, a drug dealer, a sometimes whore. And Maise wants nothing more than to not turn out like her mother. But here she is, substituting a Dad with any man she can get close to, including those who obviously want only what she offers between her legs. She knows what she's doing. She even sort of accepts it, accepts the irony. <br /><b>
  <blockquote>"Maybe it was time to admit that being wanted intensely for a few minutes wasn't enough. It got me through a few hours, a few days her and there, but when the emptiness returned it felt bigger, hungrier."</blockquote>
</b><br /><br />Until Evan....<br />The way they meet...the carnival, their moment on the roller coaster, their clandestine hookup in his Monte Carlo...it's all so junky, so trashy, so yuck. Evan's much older, but he doesn't act like her other hookups. He touches her face, kisses her gently, and makes plans to meet later. And Maise puts a stop to that shit quick. She simply doesn't show.<br /><br />Until she shows up in class...<br />And there is Mr. Wilke, her teacher.<br /><b>
  <blockquote>"On the way out the door I glanced back. Mr. Wilke watched me, his face angled partially away, shadowed. Our gazes struck like flint and steel. And I realized that gunsmoke smell wasn't ozone. It was us. We burned."</blockquote>
</b><br /><br /><b>
  <u>MY THOUGHTS</u>
</b><br />And so begins this messed up tale of a forbidden affair. Let me tell you, I was really weirded out for the first twenty percent of this book. I couldn't get into the sex scenes, because I was too busy feeling icky and feeling sorry for Maise. The girl has obvious issues. Just because she seemed mature and was well aware of her issues doesn't mean that she wasn't being taken advantage of. <br /><br />At NO POINT in this story did I think that Evan was doing the right thing. At no point did I really ever see this as some epic romance novel. However, I can understand the fallibility of being human, the way that a person can...if not justify...then pacify their own conscience into ignoring right and wrong. By the time that Evan realizes how deep into the shit he is, he also realizes that Maise needs SOMEONE. I know, I know that it's messed up that her only someone comes in the form of an old dude, a teacher, no less, who also sleeps with her. But his stability was actually more than she'd ever had.<br /><br />Maise also begins an odd friendship with another boy at school...these two form an unlikely bond, and betweeen him and Mr. Wilke (i.e., Evan), she begins to see the world much less critically. <br /><br />Maise begins this story so lost, so disillusioned with life, so <i>cynical</i> for her age. We never know the true depravity of what she went through as a young girl, but with a Mother like hers, there is much alluded to, and it ain't pretty. <br /><br /><b>
  <blockquote>"Who fixes broken people? Is it only other broken people, ones who've already been ruined? And do we need to be fixed? It was the messiness and hurt in our pasts that drove us, and that same hurt connected us at a subdermal level, the kind o scars written so deeply in your cells that you can't even see them any more, only recognize them in someone else.."</blockquote>
</b><br /><br />One of the things that I found most wonderful about this story was how Maise never blamed others for her situation. THIS IS NOT A WHINY, BITCHY HEROINE. Maise is the kind of person that I really want to root for. She stands behind her actions. She deals with consequences. She is young but not stupid, naïve but not a doormat. She accepts her faults, she face-palms her damned self, and she moves forward...always forward, (minus a much deserved meltdown). <i>Evan will most definitely NOT make it to my favorite heroes shelf, but it's beyond my better judgement that I put Maise on my favorite heroine shelf. She effing rules.</i><br /><br />I can keep going, and I have pages and pages of quotes and highlights. Let me just say this: the subject matter made me a little tetchy, because at first I thought that this book was trying to manipulate me into admitting that an affair between a 33 year old man and his 18 year old student was yummy in that taboo kind of way. And I don't think that was the intent at all. What I took from this story is so much more than some lascivious, naughty little adventure. This author has a very lyrical voice, a romantic soul...and not only the hearts and flowers romance. It's real life and it's hard knocks and it's not always pretty. It's crappy family and forced friendships and it's love that's both wrong and<br /><br />Oh..<br />So...<br />Right.<br /><br />(I may edit this later. I am off on vacation and tapping this out while I'm heading out the door.)</span>
  <a data-text-id="16060699226195922564" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

          </span>
        </div>

<div id="review_679579605" class="review nosyndicate" itemprop="reviews" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Review">
  <link itemprop="url" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/679579605" />
    <a title="* Meli Mel *" class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/10905711-meli-mel"><img alt="* Meli Mel *" src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1577750127p2/10905711.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/679579605?book_show_action=true">Jul 28, 2013</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="* Meli Mel *" class="user" itemprop="url" name="* Meli Mel *" href="/user/show/10905711-meli-mel">* Meli Mel *</a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="it was amazing"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">it was amazing</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span></span>

          <span class="greyText">&nbsp;&middot;&nbsp;</span>
          <a class="lightGreyText" title="Kindle Edition " href="/book/show/17978680-unteachable">review of another edition</a>


        

          <div class="uitext greyText bookshelves">
            Shelves:
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/10905711-meli-mel?shelf=female-pov">female-pov</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/10905711-meli-mel?shelf=favorites">favorites</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/10905711-meli-mel?shelf=forbidden-love">forbidden-love</a>
          </div>
    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer679579605" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer3727607687157522346"><img src='https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1380430897i/864163._SX540_.jpg' width='125' class='gr-hostedUserImg'/><br/><b>♥♥♥ 4.5 Forbidden Stars ♥♥♥</b><br/><br/><img src='https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1445452828ra/16652293.gif' width='400' class='gr-hostedUserImg'/><br/><br/><blockquote>
  <b>
    <i>●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●<br/><br/>"You asked why I'm here alone."<br/><br/>I glanced over at him. He stared right ahead.<br/><br/>"I see the lights every night. It seems like the whole world has figured out how to be happy, but no one's letting me in on the secret." <br/><br/>●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●</i>
  </b>
</blockquote><br/><img src='https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1379794785i/596848._SX540_.jpg' width='405' class='gr-hostedUserImg'/><br/><br/>Maise O'Malley has just turned eighteen. She is not the sweet-girl-next-door kind of girl. She hasn't been that for a long time. She is confiden</span>
  <span id="freeText3727607687157522346" style="display:none"><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1380430897i/864163._SX540_.jpg" width="125" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><b>♥♥♥ 4.5 Forbidden Stars ♥♥♥</b><br><br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1445452828ra/16652293.gif" width="400" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br><blockquote>
  <b>
    <i>●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●<br><br>"You asked why I'm here alone."<br><br>I glanced over at him. He stared right ahead.<br><br>"I see the lights every night. It seems like the whole world has figured out how to be happy, but no one's letting me in on the secret." <br><br>●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●</i>
  </b>
</blockquote><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1379794785i/596848._SX540_.jpg" width="405" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>Maise O'Malley has just turned eighteen. She is not the sweet-girl-next-door kind of girl. She hasn't been that for a long time. She is confident, promiscious, and alone. Her childhood was non-exitent. She has been taking care of her junkie mother and herself since she was very young. Her father abandoned them and now she has daddy issues. But all she wants is to forget for a little while. So, she sleeps with older men to accomplish it. Things change for her when she meets a man at the carnival. After, sleeping with him, he looks at her as more than just a body to get relief from, he looks at her like wants to see all of her. But she is not after anything more than just sex. When school finally starts, she is stunned to find out that the man she slept with, is her teacher.<br><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1379794785i/596848._SX540_.jpg" width="405" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br><br>This book was <b>so</b> different from your typical <b>Teacher-Student- forbidden-love</b> story. As soon as I started reading, I <b>couldn't</b> put it down.<br><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1380430897i/864165.jpg" width="400" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br><blockquote>
  <b><i>●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●<br><br>"How do I make you feel?"<br><br></i>Alive. Real. Valuable. Whole.<i><br><br>"Like myself," I said. "More than I've ever been."<br><br>●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●</i></b>
</blockquote><br>Maise was such a <b>refreshing</b> character. She isn't a normal eighteen year old girl, that's for sure. She is a loner but doesn't mind being that way. She may even appear to be a bit stuck up, but it's just a shield she uses to let no one in. I really liked her. At times she seems wiser than her age because of the things she has gone through growing up, with her mother being a <b>prostitute</b> and <b>drug addict</b>. But in the end, she was still a kid. She had also been sexually active for quite a while. She is messed up completely and definitely has <b>"daddy issues"</b> like she always kept mentioning. She seeks out older men to sleep with, sometimes <b>twice</b> or <b>three times</b> her senior. All she wants is to forget her reality, and sex seems to be her cure, for a while at least. I liked how she worked to make what she <b>wanted</b> to happen near the end and how she seemed to pick herself up when life threw her down.<br><br><blockquote>
  <b>
    <i>●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●<br><br>"You're so alive, Maise. You're so here, so present in the moment. You've taught me that happiness is possible now, not in some distant future. You'll scale a mountain without a second thought, face your fears, throw yourself into danger, and you're not reckless but bold, proud. You have a lion's heart. You're not afraid to live." <br><br>●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●</i>
  </b>
</blockquote><br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1380222758ra/616137.gif" width="400" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>Having sex with a stranger in his car at the carnival, makes her feel things she can't describe. That is because she <b>doesn't</b> really know what love is, or what <b>real affection</b> feels like. She had always just felt pleasure and was left with a kind of high after having sex. But now she feels <b>scared</b> by the way she is feeling after the stranger, Evan, says he doesn't want just a one night stand, he wants to get to <b>know</b> her. It <b>terrifies</b> her, so she leaves him with an excuse of using the restroom, only to see him again, when she goes to her film class. She finds out Evan, is Mr. Wilke, her <b>teacher</b>. Legally, they can be together because she is now eighteen, but since she is his student, they can't. I liked that she didn't act like a crazy after finding out. She acted <b>reasonable</b> and accepted what happened <b>without</b> whining about it. <br><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1380430897i/864166._SX540_.jpg" width="400" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br><blockquote>
  <b><i>●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●<br><br>“Maise," he said, "I love you."<br><br></i>I love you, I thought (...) You made the world come alive for me and I love you, I love you, I love you. But it was so hard to get the air out my lungs, and then he kissed me, and I stopped trying. <br><br>●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●</b>
</blockquote><br>Evan Wilke was a thirty-two year old man who seemed to be <b>caring</b> and <b>sincere</b> from the moment you met him. He never blamed Maise for sleeping with him without knowing her real age. In fact, he was ready to give it <b>all</b> up if that's what she wanted. But Maise asked him to stay. They could no longer hold back, and so, an <b>affair</b> ensued. Evan was a bit of a mystery. He wanted to know Maise, but we didn't really <b>know</b> him. Evan was holding back and ended up keeping a very <b>big</b> secret from her. Evan acted way younger then his age at times. I think it's because of the trauma he suffered from his upbringing. He needed to <b>grow</b> up in a sense just like Maise needed too. That is why they were so good together. They brought out the <b>good</b> stuff out of each other and were learning <b>together</b>.<br><br><blockquote>
  <b>
    <i>●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●<br><br>"Don't be afraid," Evan said. "We're in this together, hand in hand, against the world," <br><br>●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●</i>
  </b>
</blockquote><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1380430897i/864167.jpg" width="400" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>I really liked the supporting characters. Wesley <b>stole</b> my heart as the guy with a big crush on Maise. He was a <b>loner</b> as well, and also interested in film like Maise. He became Maise's <b>only</b> friend. He was one of the few people who really <b>understood</b> and <b>cared</b> about Maise. They both had <b>similar</b> ways of seeing things but also didn't see eye to eye on many things. Wesley, like Maise and Evan, were people who were <b>lost</b>. They are still trying to figure out <b>who</b> they are, <b>what</b> they want, <b>how</b> to let go of their demons, and how to <b>live</b>. Maise and Evan became confused about their relationship. They both knew that because it was <b>forbidden</b>, it added to the excitement of being together, so they needed to figure out if what they felt was <b>real</b>, because soon, it would no longer be forbidden.<br><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1380430897i/864168.jpg" width="400" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br><blockquote>
  <b>
    <i>●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●<br><br>"You changed my life, Mr. Wilke."<br><br>His arms tightened around me, and he whispered back, "You changed mine."<br><br>●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●</i>
  </b>
</blockquote><br>The writing was <b>fabulous</b>. I can't stress that enough... <b>Amazing!</b> It was such a <b>unique</b> read but very <b>enjoyable</b>. It was love story but there was so much more to it. And of course, there was plenty of <b>steam</b>. It was really <b>HOT</b>! It was <b>not</b> a fairy-tale, but a story that depicted a forbidden relationship in a <b>realistic</b> manner. I wasn't sure how the ending would be like, but I ended up pleased with the conclusion. I just would have liked there to have been an epilogue, but that's just my preference. If you <b>don't</b> like books about taboo subjects, than this is not for you. I really <b>loved</b> this book. I definitely recommend you give this a read.<br><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1379794785i/596848._SX540_.jpg" width="405" class="gr-hostedUserImg"></span>
  <a data-text-id="3727607687157522346" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

          </span>
        </div>

    <a title="La-Lionne" class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/11644154-la-lionne"><img alt="La-Lionne" src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1458815714p2/11644154.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/680181142?book_show_action=true">Jul 29, 2013</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="La-Lionne" class="user" itemprop="url" name="La-Lionne" href="/user/show/11644154-la-lionne">La-Lionne</a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="liked it"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">liked it</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span></span>

          <span class="greyText">&nbsp;&middot;&nbsp;</span>
          <a class="lightGreyText" title="Kindle Edition " href="/book/show/17978680-unteachable">review of another edition</a>


        

          <div class="uitext greyText bookshelves">
            Shelves:
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/11644154-la-lionne?shelf=action-packed">action-packed</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/11644154-la-lionne?shelf=bad-girl">bad-girl</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/11644154-la-lionne?shelf=forbidden-love">forbidden-love</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/11644154-la-lionne?shelf=hot">hot</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/11644154-la-lionne?shelf=kinky">kinky</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/11644154-la-lionne?shelf=sweet">sweet</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/11644154-la-lionne?shelf=sexy">sexy</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/11644154-la-lionne?shelf=tough-ass-heroine">tough-ass-heroine</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/11644154-la-lionne?shelf=frustrating">frustrating</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/11644154-la-lionne?shelf=bad-boy">bad-boy</a>
          </div>
    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer680181142" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer10953281774091525109"><b>***3 forbidden stars***</b><br/><br/><img src='https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1380430980i/864487.jpg' width='300' height='500' alt='description' class='gr-hostedUserImg'/><br/><br/>Here is the thing. I loved the book for the fact that it was a hard-to-put-it-down-er, it's fast paced and brilliantly written, I read it in one sitting with only a short nap in between :-). But, and it's a big but, I had one huge issue with the story, which was a deal breaker for me and the main reason for me giving 3 stars. I'll get back to it.<br/><br/>- - - WARNING, MAJOR SPOILERS AHEAD - - -<br/><br/><b>Maise:</b><br/>Loved her at the beginning. She is funny, gritty and sarcastic. She is smart (for </span>
  <span id="freeText10953281774091525109" style="display:none"><b>***3 forbidden stars***</b><br><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1380430980i/864487.jpg" width="300" height="500" alt="description" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>Here is the thing. I loved the book for the fact that it was a hard-to-put-it-down-er, it's fast paced and brilliantly written, I read it in one sitting with only a short nap in between :-). But, and it's a big but, I had one huge issue with the story, which was a deal breaker for me and the main reason for me giving 3 stars. I'll get back to it.<br><br>- - - WARNING, MAJOR SPOILERS AHEAD - - -<br><br><b>Maise:</b><br>Loved her at the beginning. She is funny, gritty and sarcastic. She is smart (for her age), but she is also a girl with a lot of daddy issues that f@cked her up big time, and sometimes, she doesn't know her left foot from her right foot. She jumps from one older guy to another, looking for love in all the wrong places. That's how she meets Evan. <br><br>It's all fun and games at first, until it's not. They have a lot of good moments, fun conversations and oh-so hot encounters. Until... Until they find out that he is a teacher and she is his student. It's still fun, the secret glances, barely-there touches, the stolen kisses and secret meetings... Maise is over the moon, it's exiting. <br><br><b>Evan:</b><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1380430980i/864488._SX540_.jpg" width="400" height="250" alt="description" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br>Now this one is an exotic fruit, who has barely legal girl fetish. The younger, the better. I know it sounds sick, but that's how I saw him. He has a history of getting involved with his students. What? You say it was only two girls? I say it's two girls too many.<br>I liked him at first. I actually thought that as wrong as their relationship was, it was sweet, romantic and fun. Until his secret came out about him getting involved with a 17 year old student in his previous job. I wanted to kick myself for like him. <br><b>
  <blockquote>"I had a relationship with a student," he said.<br>(...)<br>"A highschool girl," I said.<br>"Yes."<br>"How old?"<br>He sighed, long and deep. His shoulders had a concave, defensive arc. "Seventeen when it started. Eighteen when it ended."<br>(...)<br>"She was infatuated with me. And I made a huge mistake in returning it."<br>
</blockquote>
</b> No shit, Sherlock! <br>After this, I couldn't look at his character the same way, and all of their previous encounters didn't look fun, romantic or hot anymore. I saw him as a man abusing his position to get his rocks of with a young girl. <br><br><b>Wes:</b><br>In the middle of all that we have Wes. I absolutely loved him, even more so after he showed his movie. His character sparked quite a discussion amongst my GR friends, which was fun :-). I came to a conclusion that if you love Evan and Maise, you will hate Wes, and if you love Wes, you will hate Evan and Maise :-). <br>I thought he used his project as a last resort to show Maise how wrong her relationship with Evan was. Yes, his method was a bit harsh, but desperate times called for desperate measures. It was said that he betrayed their friendship and humiliated her. I thought he did no such thing, because of the way he made his movie. Only those involved knew what that movie was about. It's not like he revealed to the whole class that she was sleeping with her teacher. Plus, he gave her numerous opportunities to come and talk to him, which she did not. Maise wasn't without a fault either. She lied to Wes over and over again. He opened his heart and his home to her, introduced her to his family who embraced her with open arms, and that's how she repaid him? While she was getting cosy with his mother and sister, she was lying her butt off, and Wes knew that. If you were in Wes's position and a friend was doing something like that to you, how would that make you feel?<br><br><b>Bottom line:</b><br><br>Maise kept saying that she learned a lot from her relationship with Evan. What exactly did she learned? <br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1380430980i/864489._SX540_.png" width="400" height="250" alt="description" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br>At the end Maise was the same Maise I met on the first page: a girl looking for attention from older man, because she haven't gotten that from her father. Is that why this book is called Unteachable?<br><br>I would have given 5 stars if it wasn't for the fact that Evan had an affair with 17 tear old student. That made him look like he has a pattern of seducing his students, made him look like an old pervert with taste for young flesh. I also hate the fact that they end up together. I don't believe they were in love. I saw them as two people with a lot of issues using each other to fill the void that other people in their lives left. I can easily imagine Evan after couple of years drooling over yet another of his students, because Maise became too old for him. He did say that her being young is the big part of why he liked her. What happens when she gets older? I'm sure he will go looking for another young thing.<br><br>All and all, I loved the writing, it was fast paced and hard to put it down. I'll defiantly be reading the next book by this author. <br><br><i>Thanks for reading it with me, <a href="https://www.goodreads.com/user/show/11057966-alex" rel="nofollow noopener">Alex</a>. Good times :-).<br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1380430980ra/864490.gif" width="400" height="300" alt="description" class="gr-hostedUserImg"></i></span>
  <a data-text-id="10953281774091525109" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

              <span id="reviewTextContainer679920128" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer3950743443842258855"><b>5 Absolutely Beautiful Forbidden Stars</b><br/><img src='https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1380430944i/864366._SY540_.jpg' class='gr-hostedUserImg'/><br/><b>
  <i>"I don't know what I'm doing with you."<br/>"That's okay, just don't stop."</i>
</b><br/><img src='https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1380430944i/864367._SX540_.jpg' class='gr-hostedUserImg'/><br/><img src='https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1380430944i/864368.jpg' class='gr-hostedUserImg'/><br/><br/>Have you ever began reading a book, and just a few sentences in you knew...you just knew that this was going to be unlike anything you have ever read before? Unteachable was that book for me. I was sucked in from just the few first words, and it didn't let me up until the very last page.<br/><br/>To say that Leah Raedar has a gift for words and story telling would be a gross understatement. The </span>
  <span id="freeText3950743443842258855" style="display:none"><b>5 Absolutely Beautiful Forbidden Stars</b><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1380430944i/864366._SY540_.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><b>
  <i>"I don't know what I'm doing with you."<br>"That's okay, just don't stop."</i>
</b><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1380430944i/864367._SX540_.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1380430944i/864368.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>Have you ever began reading a book, and just a few sentences in you knew...you just knew that this was going to be unlike anything you have ever read before? Unteachable was that book for me. I was sucked in from just the few first words, and it didn't let me up until the very last page.<br><br>To say that Leah Raedar has a gift for words and story telling would be a gross understatement. The writing was one of the best parts of this book. Leah weaves words together so seamlessly and effortlessly that the words blur into images in your mind. The entire book unfolds before you like a movie, and IT.WAS.INCREDIBLE!<br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1380430944ra/864369.gif" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>Maise O'Malley is not your typical happy-go-lucky, soon to be high school senior. She's an old soul, in the body of an 18 year old girl. She's broken, but she knows it. She hasn't exactly had it easy in life, and her family or lack thereof is anything to brag about. She has a void that she fills with meaningless sex with faceless, older men. And it makes her feel...something...if only for those few too-short minutes. <br><blockquote>
  <b>Thanks, Dad, for leaving a huge void in my life that Freud says has to be filled with dick.</b>
</blockquote><br>But then one late summer night spent at a local carnival Maise met the one man that will change everything. Evan Wilke. <br><br>A steamy encounter in his car later, Maise knows that Evan is not going to be just another faceless memory.<br><blockquote>
  <b>The funny thing was that his kiss had felt like fucking me, and his fucking me felt like being kissed, everywhere, every bit of my body unbearably warm and buzzing.</b>
</blockquote><br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1380430944ra/864370.gif" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>Unable to face the feelings that Evan and their night together brought out in her, Maise does the only things she can. She runs.<br>What neither of them know, is that their world is about to collide in a way that both of them least expect.<br><br>When Maise walks into class on her first day of her senior year, the man she knew as Evan on that summer night, is now Mr. Wilke, her teacher.<br><br>What began as an innocent encounter between two people finding a connection, turns into a forbidden affair.<br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1380430944i/864371._SY540_.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><blockquote>
  <b>"I can't hold on to you. You're like that shooting star. Just a trail of fire in my hands."</b>
</blockquote><br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1380430944ra/864372.gif" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>Evan clearly cares for Maise. He isn't your typical NA asshole hero. But while he's sweet and caring, he is still clearly hiding some dark secrets from his own past.<br><blockquote>
  <b>"Now I know," he said, touching me again, "why I was drawn to you. We have the same darkness inside."<br>"Our fucked-up parents?"<br>"Our lost childhood."</b>
</blockquote><br><br>Even though the odds are stacked against them, and they're risking everything if they get caught, the connection between Evan and Maise is intense. Their relationship soon stops being only a physical connection, as Evan slowly begins to chip away at the defenses around Maise's heart.<br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1380430944ra/864373.gif" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>The chemistry between them was absolutely scorching, and the steaminess in this book was off the charts for a NA novel.<br><blockquote>
  <b>"Who am I to you?" I asked, my voice hoarse. "Maise or your student?"<br>"Both," he whispered.<br>I felt chills.<br>"Then fuck me Mr. Wilke."</b>
</blockquote><br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1380430944ra/864374.gif" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><blockquote>
  <b>“I want to fuck you in this classroom,” I said. <br>He exhaled slowly through his teeth. <br>“On this desk,” I said. “While you’re wearing your shirt and tie, and I’m wearing nothing but socks.” <br>He kissed me to make me stop talking.</b>
</blockquote><br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1380430944ra/864375.gif" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>Their journey together is not an easy one. They face not only the demons from their own pasts, but the obstacles stacked against them; the risk of being found out.<br><br>Beautifully written, Unteachable takes you on a roller coaster of emotions.<br><br>I cannot recommend this book enough. Even if you don't typically read the New Adult genre, this is a must read. It is not the typically angsty plot with an asshole broken hero, and a naive and virginal heroine.<br><br><br>For more reviews visit: <a href="http://dirtygirlromance.blogspot.com/" rel="nofollow noopener"> Dirty Girl Romance Book Blog </a><br><br><br></span>

<div id="review_684715856" class="review nosyndicate" itemprop="reviews" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Review">
  <link itemprop="url" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/684715856" />
    <a title="• Lisa •" class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/11963959-lisa"><img alt="• Lisa •" src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1576172089p2/11963959.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/684715856?book_show_action=true">Aug 03, 2013</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="• Lisa •" class="user" itemprop="url" name="• Lisa •" href="/user/show/11963959-lisa">• Lisa •</a>
      </span>

          added it


          <span class="greyText">&nbsp;&middot;&nbsp;</span>
          <a class="lightGreyText" title="Kindle Edition " href="/book/show/17978680-unteachable">review of another edition</a>


        

          <div class="uitext greyText bookshelves">
            Shelves:
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/11963959-lisa?shelf=not-for-me-didn-t-finish">not-for-me-didn-t-finish</a>
          </div>
    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer684715856" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer5975297570871955809"><br/><b>NO STAR RATING FOR A BEAUTIFULLY PUT TOGETHER BOOK ...</b><br/><br/><img src='https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1380431619i/866226._SY540_.jpg' width='400' alt='description' class='gr-hostedUserImg'/><br/><br/>Sadly this time 'unteachable' was not for me, I have refrained from rating, I don't believe in a reader rating a book unless they have finished the whole story. I felt disappointed that I was unable to finish, almost like the kid who showed up at the party not knowing it was a fancy dress theme. On the one hand The author deserves five stars for her gorgeously written book but unfortunately, me and this book were not meant to be.<br/><br/>'Unteachable'</span>
  <span id="freeText5975297570871955809" style="display:none"><br><b>NO STAR RATING FOR A BEAUTIFULLY PUT TOGETHER BOOK ...</b><br><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1380431619i/866226._SY540_.jpg" width="400" alt="description" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>Sadly this time 'unteachable' was not for me, I have refrained from rating, I don't believe in a reader rating a book unless they have finished the whole story. I felt disappointed that I was unable to finish, almost like the kid who showed up at the party not knowing it was a fancy dress theme. On the one hand The author deserves five stars for her gorgeously written book but unfortunately, me and this book were not meant to be.<br><br>'Unteachable' is written to lovingly poetic proportions, there is a difference to the authors writing style that is rare and compelling. The book flowed so well and easy I found myself going from chapter to chapter with ease. Sadly around the 35% mark I started to feel uncomfortable with what I was reading and made the decision to stop at that point.<br><br><b>So why DNF you might ask?</b><br>Whilst I can not take away the authors outstanding ability to put together words like magic I struggled with the content. You may want to say to me that I knew what I was signing up for starting this book, and the obvious answer to that it is, YES but I could not have predicted how I felt once I got to know the characters. I struggled with the vulnerability of the leading female character and that pulled me towards feeling uncomfortable with the content I was reading.<br><br><b>Final thoughts ...</b><br>I hope this author writes future stories that I can engage with because their is no doubt in my mind that Leah Raeder is talented beyond words. This story has taken readers on GoodReads by storm, so if you like extraordinary talented writing that showcases a taboo subject that will undoubtably get your heart racing then go grab the story of Maise O'Malley and Evan. Enjoy readers, kisses ...</span>
  <a data-text-id="5975297570871955809" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

          </span>

<span id="freeTextContainer16028515075967443603"><b>
  <i>“I can’t hold on to you. You’re like that shooting star. Just a trail of fire in my hands.”</i>
</b><br/><br/><u>
  <i>4.5 Stars!</i>
</u><br/><br/>As soon as I finished this book, the first thing was my brain said was <b>WOW</b><br/>Yupp, my brain totally said that. This book was <b>AMAZING. Like brilliant and amazing.</b> Some parts of the book were very cliché and it bugged the living shit out of me; but apart from all of that this book was still <b>WOW</b><br/><br/>It was written is such a beautiful manner; very very poetic! I totally lost myself in the book. <b>Each </b></span>
  <span id="freeText16028515075967443603" style="display:none"><b>
  <i>“I can’t hold on to you. You’re like that shooting star. Just a trail of fire in my hands.”</i>
</b><br><br><u>
  <i>4.5 Stars!</i>
</u><br><br>As soon as I finished this book, the first thing was my brain said was <b>WOW</b><br>Yupp, my brain totally said that. This book was <b>AMAZING. Like brilliant and amazing.</b> Some parts of the book were very cliché and it bugged the living shit out of me; but apart from all of that this book was still <b>WOW</b><br><br>It was written is such a beautiful manner; very very poetic! I totally lost myself in the book. <b>Each page blended into the other and I just didn't want to keep it down.</b><br><br><b>This book has some AMAZING and extremely touching and beautiful quotes.</b>I have so many highlighted. And I am so getting a tattoo of one of them when I start inking my body~<br><br>Maise was very very unique. My type of a girl. Spoke about anything and everything and always spilled what the fuck ever was on her mind. Loved her.<br><br>Evan in one word was HOT!!<br><br>They met in the carnival of all the places...<br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1380430897ra/864164.gif" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br><b>
  <i>“I see the lights every night. It seems like the whole world has figured out how to be happy, but no one’s letting me in on the secret.”</i>
</b><br><br>Two sad souls met and completed each other.<br><br><b>
  <i>You can call it love, or you can call it freefall. They’re pretty much the same thing.</i>
</b><br><br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1380428278ra/856838.gif" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>They got off on each other, on their age gap, their titles, on everything life had to give them.<br><br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1380222758ra/616137.gif" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br><b>
  <i>“We have no age. We exist outside of time. We’re timeless.”</i>
</b><br><br>They both fought to achieve what they are and where they are and where they will go in the tomorrow.<br><br><b>
  <i>And I realized that gunsmoke smell wasn’t ozone. It was us. We burned.</i>
</b><br><br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1380416419ra/822369.gif" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br><i>“The night I met you was like someone handed me a winning lottery ticket and said, ‘You can only have it if you don’t tell anyone.’”</i><br><br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1380431339ra/865448.gif" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>Do read this book. It is AMAZING!!! :D<br><br><b>The author's writing style - Giving it 5✩s would be giving it far too less!!<br>It was captivating! Every sentence written oozed Opium.<br><br>Cant wait to see what else Leah Raeder has to offer! Because I'm so getting in line and waiting</b></span>

<div id="review_1081549282" class="review" itemprop="reviews" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Review">
  <link itemprop="url" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/1081549282" />
    <a title="Jasmine" class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/31339793-jasmine"><img alt="Jasmine" src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1406624675p2/31339793.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/1081549282?book_show_action=true">Oct 16, 2014</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="Jasmine" class="user" itemprop="url" name="Jasmine" href="/user/show/31339793-jasmine">Jasmine</a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="really liked it"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">really liked it</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span></span>

          <span class="greyText">&nbsp;&middot;&nbsp;</span>
          <a class="lightGreyText" title="Kindle Edition " href="/book/show/17978680-unteachable">review of another edition</a>


          <div>
    <span class="greyText">Recommended to Jasmine by: </span>
      <a href="/user/show/16349243-saffron">Saffron</a>
  </div>


          <div class="uitext greyText bookshelves">
            Shelves:
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/31339793-jasmine?shelf=buddy-recs">buddy-recs</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/31339793-jasmine?shelf=smartass-witty-banters">smartass-witty-banters</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/31339793-jasmine?shelf=forbidden-taboo-love">forbidden-taboo-love</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/31339793-jasmine?shelf=new-adult">new-adult</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/31339793-jasmine?shelf=oh-look-pretty-cover">oh-look-pretty-cover</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/31339793-jasmine?shelf=favorites">favorites</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/31339793-jasmine?shelf=i-love-me-some-angst-drama">i-love-me-some-angst-drama</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/31339793-jasmine?shelf=imma-hit-that-bitch">imma-hit-that-bitch</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/31339793-jasmine?shelf=panty-soaking-wet">panty-soaking-wet</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/31339793-jasmine?shelf=standalones">standalones</a>
          </div>
    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer1081549282" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer15918076372056804139"><b>4.5 UNTEACHABLE STARS ★★★★☆</b><br/><br/><img src='https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1413659849i/11541585.jpg' class='gr-hostedUserImg'/><br/><br/><b>
  <i>“You can call it love, or you can call it freefall. They're pretty much the same thing.”</i>
</b><br/><br/>Once again I find myself living under a huge rock when I found out that I've never heard of this read until one of of my lovely GR buddies rec'd this one to me. I know, don't get shocked but this is actually my first real teacher/student read and after this one, I'm wondering where I've been all my life because sign me up for more!<br/><br/><img src='https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1413656719ra/11541117.gif' class='gr-hostedUserImg'/><br/><br/>*******<br/><br/><b>Unteachable</b> starts off with our heroine, </span>
  <span id="freeText15918076372056804139" style="display:none"><b>4.5 UNTEACHABLE STARS ★★★★☆</b><br><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1413659849i/11541585.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br><b>
  <i>“You can call it love, or you can call it freefall. They're pretty much the same thing.”</i>
</b><br><br>Once again I find myself living under a huge rock when I found out that I've never heard of this read until one of of my lovely GR buddies rec'd this one to me. I know, don't get shocked but this is actually my first real teacher/student read and after this one, I'm wondering where I've been all my life because sign me up for more!<br><br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1413656719ra/11541117.gif" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>*******<br><br><b>Unteachable</b> starts off with our heroine, <b>Maise: an Irish, 18-year old student who acts and thinks beyond her age due to her troubled upbringing</b>; growing up without a dad and also having to care for her mother who is a druggie. <br><br><i>
  <blockquote>"Thanks, Dad, for leaving a huge void in my life that Freud says has to be filled with dick."</blockquote>
</i><br>But <b>one night at the carnival changed everything for two people</b> when Maise took a ride on the Deathsnake and sat next to a stranger. Unbeknownst to them, this was the ride that catapulted them into a tale of forbidden love.<br><br>With undeniable sparks that flew between them and after a hot sex session in the car that night, Maise soon discovered that that stranger is not just another faceless memory but is in fact <b>32-year old, Mr. Evan Wilkes who will be her teacher in senior year.</b> <br><br>********<br><br>Let me just say that the <b>writing is phenomenal</b>. Stepping into this book, I was surprised to see this <b>unique lyrical-like prose</b> that the author brought which I found to be so beautiful and captivating to read. Although told entirely from Maise's POV, I felt that the forbidden aspect was still captured perfectly and how fast I found myself to be so consumed by this emotionally powerful read.<br><br><i>
  <blockquote>“There's something so terrible about wanting something you've already had. You know exactly what you're missing. Your body knows precisely how to shape itself around the ache, the hollowness that wants to be filled”</blockquote>
</i> <br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1413657916ra/11541356.gif" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>I really loved Maise's character, mostly for <b>her resilience</b> and her <b>incredible inner monologue filled with sarcasm &amp; wit</b> that had me chuckling at most times. But most of all, I really felt and hurt for this young lady to have to put up with most of the shit she's been dealing with at such a young age. Sure enough, she doesn't make the wisest decisions &amp; there are times I wanted to slap her silly. But let's just take a step back and remember <b>that no one is perfect especially at that age</b>; we all make some slip-ups which we're not proud of.<br><br><i>
  <blockquote>“It seems like the whole world has figured out how to be happy, but no one's letting me in on the secret.”</blockquote>
</i> <br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1413657916i/11541357.gif" class="gr-hostedUserImg"> <br><br>Then there's Evan of course. This is where I had to deck out half star from my full rating as I realised that I <b>never really fully embraced his character</b>. I'm not doubting his love for Maise at all but I found that the revelation of <a class="jsShowSpoiler spoilerAction">(view spoiler)</a><span class="spoilerContainer" style="display: none">[him having committed a teacher-student affair previously kinda trivialised their current rship <a class="jsHideSpoiler spoilerAction">(hide spoiler)</a>]</span> and ruined him a little for me. I honestly wished it was a different revelation that had played out.<br><br>********<br><br>Overall this read took me by a huge surprise and got me hooked from start to finish. I thought the epilogue was done beautifully and brought the story back to a full circle. Also it did a great deal on my health as it sent me on a full-on panic attack mode when things started going awry for them and I genuinely felt so scared for them. <br><br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1413658942ra/11541491.gif" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>But what I <b>really loved most</b> about the book was how easily I could <b>visualize most scenes in my head</b> and the writing was exceptional that those <b>scenes felt so vivid in my mind.</b> So much so that the scene where Maise's video project was played out felt so vivid that it brought tears to my eyes. Truly beautiful is all I can say ♥ <br><br>I definitely highly recommend this read if you're looking for a powerful, gritty read that touches on this student/teacher premise and is looking to get a taste of some exquisite writing :) </["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></span>
  <a data-text-id="15918076372056804139" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

          </span>

<div id="review_1188489769" class="review nosyndicate" itemprop="reviews" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Review">
  <link itemprop="url" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/1188489769" />
    <a title="✘✘ Sarah ✘✘ (former Nefarious Breeder of Murderous Crustaceans)" class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/7298986-sarah-former-nefarious-breeder-of-murderous-crustaceans"><img alt="✘✘ Sarah ✘✘ (former Nefarious Breeder of Murderous Crustaceans)" src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1587115780p2/7298986.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/1188489769?book_show_action=true">Feb 02, 2015</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
