  <span id="freeText2898880599565933028" style="display:none"><b>Buddy Read with <a href="https://www.goodreads.com/user/show/25393430-sh3lly-not-all-those-who-wander-are-lost" rel="nofollow noopener">Shelly</a>, <a href="https://www.goodreads.com/user/show/31366847-jaime" rel="nofollow noopener">Jaime</a>, <a href="https://www.goodreads.com/user/show/5028851-cathryn" rel="nofollow noopener">Cathryn</a>, <a href="https://www.goodreads.com/user/show/31718503-tanya" rel="nofollow noopener">Tanya</a>, <a href="https://www.goodreads.com/user/show/31239385-lea" rel="nofollow noopener">Lea</a>, <a href="https://www.goodreads.com/user/show/13870608-jo-the-book-sloth" rel="nofollow noopener">Jo</a> &amp; <a href="https://www.goodreads.com/user/show/10336538-jessica-rabid-reads" rel="nofollow noopener">Jessica</a> starting March 6, 2015.</b><br><br><b>Because</b> I'd read just about anything with my <a href="https://www.goodreads.com/group/show/148935-dust-off-your-machalo-it-s-time-for-a-re-read" rel="nofollow noopener">MacHalo Freaks</a>. <b>And because I'm brave.</b><br><br><b>Updated March 6, 2015:</b><br><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1421966963i/13437420.gif" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br><b>✘ AND THIS IS ME SADLY BAILING OUT ON MY FAVOURITE FREAKS ✘</b><br><br><b>Because</b> I read the first chapter last night and already want to put a bullet through my head. <b>Because</b> I read the first chapter last night and already think this is one of the silliest, most ridiculous books I've ever read. <b>Because</b> I've been eyerolling so much my eyeballs are hurting. <b>Because</b> I'm tired of trying to commit book-induced suicide. <b>Because</b> I'm beginning to think I should stop trying to read books out of my comfort zone. <b>Because</b> I've read so many crappy books so far this year that I'm actually considering NOT reading for a while. And that's a really depressing thought. <b>Because</b> I don't want to put my friends through another one of my DNF graveyard reviews. <br><br><b>YES. This is really happening.</b> I'm actually DNFing a book before reaching the 10% mark. <b>This is a new low for me.</b><br><br><b>So sorry to let you down my Freaks but I just can't do this. </b><br><br><i>ETA: the lack of rating is fully intentional. I didn't make it past the 9% mark and my rating this book wouldn't be fair on either the author or her work.</i><br><br><b>Definitely <a href="https://www.goodreads.com/group/show/148935-dust-off-your-machalo-it-s-time-for-a-re-read" rel="nofollow noopener">MacHalo approved</a>. Just not for me.</b><br><br></span>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">

        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="it was amazing"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">it was amazing</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span></span>

          <a class="lightGreyText" title="Kindle Edition " href="/book/show/17978680-unteachable">review of another edition</a>


        

          <div class="uitext greyText bookshelves">
            Shelves:
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/9138738-georgia?shelf=contemporary">contemporary</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/9138738-georgia?shelf=in-love-with">in-love-with</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/9138738-georgia?shelf=sobbing-mess">sobbing-mess</a>,

              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/9138738-georgia?shelf=favourite-cause-it-is-unique">favourite-cause-it-is-unique</a>
          </div>
    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer686654676" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer13252902348333313938"><b>5 Forbidden Love, the Forever Kind Stars<br/><br/><i>"The guy and I reached for each other’s hands spontaneously and simultaneously. And I felt something I’ve never felt before. You can call it love, or you can call it freefall. They’re pretty much the same thing."</i></b><br/><br/><img src='https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1380430988i/864498.jpg' width='400' height='220' alt='description' class='gr-hostedUserImg'/><br/><br/>Love is powerful and powerless, unlimited and uncharted. It strikes you when you least expect it and when you think you don't need it, but don't be foolish. You need love. To flourish and to learn, to breathe and to live, to grow wings and let them</span>
  <span id="freeText13252902348333313938" style="display:none"><b>5 Forbidden Love, the Forever Kind Stars<br><br><i>"The guy and I reached for each other’s hands spontaneously and simultaneously. And I felt something I’ve never felt before. You can call it love, or you can call it freefall. They’re pretty much the same thing."</i></b><br><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1380430988i/864498.jpg" width="400" height="220" alt="description" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>Love is powerful and powerless, unlimited and uncharted. It strikes you when you least expect it and when you think you don't need it, but don't be foolish. You need love. To flourish and to learn, to breathe and to live, to grow wings and let them carry you away, towards infinity. Breathe, live, love.<br><br><b>
  <i>“That’s all life is. Breathing in, breathing out. The space between two breaths.”</i>
</b><br><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1380431897i/866947.jpg" width="400" height="265" alt="description" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>That's what our story is about. The courage it takes to fall in love, the guts to admit it. To break the vicious circle and run away from your parents' shadow. A girl older than her 18 years and the man who is her teacher.<br><br>And as it is the case with everything beautiful, it began in the most unexpected place.<br><br><b>
  <i>“I see the lights every night. It seems like the whole world has figured out how to be happy, but no one’s letting me in on the secret.”</i>
</b><br><br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1380430901ra/864208.gif" width="400" height="220" alt="description" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>A carnival is the perfect place to hide. To run away and be a child. The child that <b>Maise O'Malley</b> never got to be. Raised by a drug addicted and dealing mother, she knows what loneliness means. Scarred in her soul and abused, she is fearless. Life tried to bend her but Maise, courageous and brave, won't let it. <br><br><b>
  <i>“I was natural, uncultured and untamed.”</i>
</b><br><br>Cynical, witty and eons older than other teenagers, she uses men and sex. Meaningless, until a "fall" will ground her world, give her purpose and some real feelings to deal with. A chance encounter, a forbidden love, will be her forever.<br><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1380431897i/866948.jpg" width="400" height="320" alt="description" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>The mystery man that confused and awoke her senses, <b>E. Wilke</b>, her Film Studies teacher, is a man living in limbo. He knows he wants Maise, their chemistry is after all explosive, but can a forbidden passion lead anywhere? Will they let the world and their fears drive them apart? Or will they claim a future, built on their dreams and their hearts' fondest wishes? Together, outside the limits of a world that ridicules feelings and diminish love.<br><br><b>
  <i>“We have no age. We exist outside of time. We’re timeless.”</i>
</b><br><br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1380431897ra/866949.gif" width="400" height="190" alt="description" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1380431897i/866950._SX540_.jpg" width="400" height="400" alt="description" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>Beautiful, captivating and enticing, this story a treat for your heart and soul. Poetical and lyrical, it will move and reduce you to tears. It will engage all your senses and bring colour to a gray world, awakening desires and passion. This one is a must-read. A book about forbidden love that isn't about power play. It's about life experiences and dreams, about what the heart needs and human nature in all it's brutally honest glory: Obsession, Addiction, Relationships. And what it remains when you leave the mystery and the uniqueness out of the equation.<br><br><b>
  <i>“If our relationship was based on forbiddenness, what would happen when it was no longer forbidden?”</i>
</b><br><br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1380431897ra/866951.gif" width="400" height="208" alt="description" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>E. and Maise will earn a place in your heart, rooting for them and despairing along with them. Just like with old movies, just as it is with their favourite <i>"Casablanca"</i>, you will pray that they will end up together. Will they? As it is in life, so it is in movies and in books; All will be resolved in the end.<br><br>A great story about love and forgiveness. Not others; first and foremost, yourself. Highly recommended, it deserves your attention. You will love it!<br><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1380431897i/866952.jpg" width="400" height="250" alt="description" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br></span>
  <a data-text-id="13252902348333313938" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

<div id="review_685533281" class="review nosyndicate" itemprop="reviews" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Review">
  <link itemprop="url" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/685533281" />
    <a title="Marina" class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/13500406-marina"><img alt="Marina" src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1361224250p2/13500406.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/685533281?book_show_action=true">Aug 04, 2013</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="Marina" class="user" itemprop="url" name="Marina" href="/user/show/13500406-marina">Marina</a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="it was amazing"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">it was amazing</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span></span>

          <span class="greyText">&nbsp;&middot;&nbsp;</span>
          <a class="lightGreyText" title="Kindle Edition " href="/book/show/17978680-unteachable">review of another edition</a>


        

          <div class="uitext greyText bookshelves">
            Shelves:
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/13500406-marina?shelf=contemporary-fiction">contemporary-fiction</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/13500406-marina?shelf=in-one-word-good">in-one-word-good</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/13500406-marina?shelf=erotic-romance">erotic-romance</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/13500406-marina?shelf=heart-stopping">heart-stopping</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/13500406-marina?shelf=food-for-thought">food-for-thought</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/13500406-marina?shelf=favorites">favorites</a>
          </div>
    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer685533281" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer6773622722542952908"><blockquote>
  <i>
    <b>“What’s it feel like?” <br/>“Remember when you thought I was jumping off to kill myself?” He winced. “It’s like that,” I said. “But no one catches you. You’re just hanging over infinity.”</b>
  </i>
</blockquote><br/><br/><br/>What's it feel like?<br/>Peaking into someone's soul like this?<br/>I'll tell you.<br/>You wonder whether you should feel sorry for this kind of f*cked up life you had to pull through. Or thank every day for being alive while feeling alive and not just numbingly going through cinematographic cuts of your existence.<br/><br/><br/><img src='https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1380431737i/866578._SY540_.jpg' class='gr-hostedUserImg'/><br/><br/><br/>You h</span>
  <span id="freeText6773622722542952908" style="display:none"><blockquote>
  <i>
    <b>“What’s it feel like?” <br>“Remember when you thought I was jumping off to kill myself?” He winced. “It’s like that,” I said. “But no one catches you. You’re just hanging over infinity.”</b>
  </i>
</blockquote><br><br><br>What's it feel like?<br>Peaking into someone's soul like this?<br>I'll tell you.<br>You wonder whether you should feel sorry for this kind of f*cked up life you had to pull through. Or thank every day for being alive while feeling alive and not just numbingly going through cinematographic cuts of your existence.<br><br><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1380431737i/866578._SY540_.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br><br>You have read about the teacher-student theme time and again.<br>You mostly know what to expect.<br>Now take all of that and rip it in half.<br>You won't find any of that here. You will find so much more.<br>Passion in the smallest of gestures.<br>Desperation filling the brinks of overflowing souls.<br>Obsession in a tangling dance with need.<br>Addiction in it's purest form.<br>Love. Raw and pulsing. Alive.<br><br><br><i>
  <b>“It means I won’t risk your future, or your happiness, or your sanity.” <br>“Good thing I only have one of those.” <br>“I’m serious.” He frowned. “Which one do you have?” <br>“Happiness,” I said, and leaned over and kissed him. Vanilla and salt.He looked at me a long time when I pulled away. It wasn’t until later that I realized he’d hoped I’d say future. That’s how you know someone loves you. When they want you to be happy even in the part of your life they’ll never see.</b>
</i><br><br><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1380431737i/866579._SY540_.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br><br><i>
  <b>“I can’t hold on to you. You’re like that shooting star. Just a trail of fire in my hands.”</b>
</i><br><br><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1380431737i/866580.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br><br>You're an intruder in this story. This girl is reading her life to you, offering it on paper. But still you're intruding.<br>This is a confession. An admission of gnawing emotions and fear.<br>Not fear of discovery. Fear of losing something alive.<br><br><br><i>
  <b>His tongue curled around mine and he kissed me like he wanted to draw out something deep, the breath from the bottom of my lungs, the blood from the innermost crypts of my heart, the essence of me.</b>
</i><br><br><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1380431737i/866581._SY540_.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br><br><i>
  <b>I love you, I thought. If I was the only person truly alive that night, it was because of you. You made the world come alive for me and I love you, I love you, I love you.</b>
</i><br><br><br>Just let yourself go and enjoy the story. Feel as you've never felt before. There is no excessive whinny background story, only hard truths and the reality of the bravest love. Jump with the girl and reach with the guy.<br><br><br><i>
  <b>When I thought I would finally collapse into myself I realized it was him, pulling at me. My skin stretched tight. My heart pressed right up against the bars of my ribs. I lay in the snow and watched the stars and even the Earth wasn’t strong enough to hold me down. A stronger gravity pulled at me. And pulled. And pulled.</b>
</i><br><br><br><i>Because at the end of the day, wouldn't you choose the front seat of a rollercoaster..?</i></span>

  function submitShelfLink(unique_id, book_id, shelf_id, shelf_name, submit_form, exclusive) {
    var checkbox_id = 'shelf_name_' + unique_id + '_' + shelf_id;
    var element = document.getElementById(checkbox_id)

    var checked = element.checked
    if (checked && exclusive) {
      // can't uncheck a radio by clicking it!
      return
    }
    if(document.getElementById("savingMessage")){
      Element.show('savingMessage')
    }
    var element_id = 'shelfInDropdownName_' + unique_id + '_' + shelf_id;
    Element.update(element_id, "saving...");
    if (submit_form) {
      Element.hide('shelfDropdown_' + unique_id)
      var form = document.getElementById('addBookForm' + book_id)
      if (form) {
        form.shelf.value = shelf_name
        form.onsubmit()
      }
    }
    else {
      var action = checked ? 'remove' : ''
      element.checked = !element.checked
      new Ajax.Request('/shelf/add_to_shelf', {asynchronous:true, evalScripts:true, onSuccess:function(request){shelfSubmitted(request, book_id, checkbox_id, element_id, unique_id, shelf_name)}, parameters:'book_id=' + book_id + '&name=' + shelf_name + '&a=' + action + '&authenticity_token=' + encodeURIComponent('7t4FemlLhuspHtRGRMY0D+lPjxkTbKpQh4JEaIK2/PvEH6Wmh1/rJF5M3wFs6fQEInsXaWdpElFf5dALwLsAVQ==')})
    }
  }

  function shelfSubmitted(request, book_id, checkbox_id, element_id, unique_id, shelf_name) {
    Element.update('shelfListfalse_' + book_id, request.responseText)
    afterShelfSave(checkbox_id, element_id, unique_id, shelf_name.escapeHTML())
  }

  function refreshGroupBox(group_id, book_id) {
    new Ajax.Updater('addGroupBooks' + book_id + '', '/group/add_book_box', {asynchronous:true, evalScripts:true, onSuccess:function(request){refreshGroupBoxComplete(request, book_id);}, parameters:'id=' + group_id + '&book_id=' + book_id + '&refresh=true' + '&authenticity_token=' + encodeURIComponent('YYZlgupo8Q+YaVhQcD1IwC9SnY2rE9sQlxyKREKq7G1LR8VeBHycwO87UxdYEojL5GYF/d8WYxFPex4nAKcQww==')})
  }

Aside from reading her brains out, she enjoys graphic design, video games, fine whiskey, and the art of self-deprecation. She lives with her very own manic pixie dream boy in Chicago.<br/><br/>(And she still writes pretentiously lyrical fiction.)</span>
